# News Archive: Elderly Care & Ageing

This appendix provides a comprehensive index of Maldivian news coverage related to elderly care, population ageing, and older persons, drawn from the archive.mv digital news archive. The archive spans from 2008 to early 2025 and includes coverage from major Dhivehi-language news outlets (Haveeru, Sun, Mihaaru, Vaguthu, Avas, Raajje, and others). Headlines are presented in the original Dhivehi alongside unofficial English translations. This index serves as a primary reference for researchers, policymakers, and development partners seeking to trace the evolution of public discourse on elderly issues in the Maldives.

**Total articles indexed: 1320**

| Date | Dhivehi Headline | English Headline (Unofficial Translation) | Link |
|---|---|---|---|
